What If?

Collection of possibilities and lost opportunites tweeted by the world.

Created for the NaNoGenMo 2014 project by @rasagy.
Created using IFTTT, Sublime Text, Excel. Formatting using HTML.
More on the project repository on Github: https://github.com/rasagy/what-if
See more such projects on the NaNoGenMo Issue list:
https://github.com/dariusk/NaNoGenMo-2014/issues
